### Physics

- `L1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{L1}}^{+,\mathrm{phys}} = P_{\mathrm{L1}} X_{\mathrm{L1}}^{-,\mathrm{phys}}, \qquad P_{\mathrm{L1}} = T_{\mathrm{phys}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{L1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{phys}}\]

  Variable legend: `X^(phys)` tracks containment geometry, phase, pressure, and seal integrity.
  Reading: structure matrix line.
  Confidence: strong

### Color and Light

### Number Theory

- `L1`
  Equation:

  \[a_{\mathrm{L1}}^+ = A_{\mathrm{L1}} a_{\mathrm{L1}}^-, \qquad A_{\mathrm{L1}} \in M_k(\mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0})\]

  Variable legend: `a` counts active resources across channels; `A_line` is an integer update matrix.
  Reading: structure matrix line.
  Confidence: strong

### Game Theory

- `L1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{L1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{L1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{L1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{L1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: structure matrix line.
  Confidence: strong
